netwerk/protocol/http/nsHttpConnection.cpp, where nsHttpConnection manages HTTP connections. When an HTTPS connection is needed, nsHttpConnection uses a TlsHandshaker object (from netwerk/protocol/http/TlsHandshaker.cpp) to initiate the TLS handshake. TlsHandshaker::SetupSSL() and TlsHandshaker::InitSSLParams() call mOwner->GetTLSSocketControl() to retrieve the TLS socket control from the underlying socket transport.\\n\\nThe nsSocketTransport (netwerk/base/nsSocketTransport2.cpp) manages the actual socket and orchestrates the addition of SSL/TLS layers through the socket provider framework. When BuildSocket() is called, it invokes provider->AddToSocket() on an nsISocketProvider for the 'ssl' or 'starttls' type, which dispatches to either nsSSLSocketProvider::AddToSocket() or nsTLSSocketProvider::AddToSocket() (both in security/manager/ssl/).\\n\\nThese providers call nsSSLIOLayerAddToSocket() (security/manager/ssl/nsNSSIOLayer.cpp), which is the critical bridge between Necko and NSS. This function:\\n1. Creates an nsSSLIOLayerHelpers object that manages intolerance tracking and TLS configuration\\n2. Creates an NSSSocketControl object to hold socket-specific TLS state\\n3. Calls nsSSLIOLayerImportFD() which invokes SSL_ImportFD() from NSS to create the SSL socket\\n4. Registers various NSS callbacks (HandshakeCallback, AuthCertificateHook, etc.)\\n5. Adds PRFileDesc I/O layers (nsSSLIOLayerIdentity and nsSSLPlaintextLayerIdentity) that intercept socket I/O\\n\\nWhen data is read/written on the socket through nsSSLIOLayerRead/nsSSLIOLayerWrite, these functions call PSMRecv/PSMSend, which delegate to the lower PRFileDesc layer (the NSS SSL socket). This triggers NSS to perform the TLS handshake.\\n\\nThe actual TLS handshake is implemented in security/nss/lib/ssl/ where:\\n- sslsecur.c contains ssl_Do1stHandshake(), which is the main handshake state machine that repeatedly calls ss->handshake() function pointers\\n- ssl3con.c contains the TLS 1.2 and earlier handshake message handlers like ssl3_SendClientHello() and ssl3_HandleServerHello()\\n\\nThis layered architecture allows Firefox's networking code to remain protocol-agnostic while delegating the complex TLS handshake implementation to NSS's cryptographic library.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":4,"cache_creation_input_tokens":609,"cache_read_input_tokens":60035,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":609},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"a4de3875-2512-4720-8b28-0fbf02e26fd2","uuid":"82ac19c6-f1c1-44ea-89b1-bffba0f9e40f"}
